***опекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опекать.html>опека́ть</a> (16475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекать.html>опека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be guardian to, to be trustee to, to have the wardship (of); to be warden to</li>
<li>to patronize; to watch over, to take care of</li></ol>

***опекун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опекун.html>опеку́н</a> (22318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекать.html>опека́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opekátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ун</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-un</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекун.html>опеку́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opekún</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекун.html>опекуна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекун.html>опекуны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекун.html>опекуно́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опеку́нша</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опеку́нский</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guardian, trustee, patron</li></ol>

***опенок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опёнок</a> (18598)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пень.html>пень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">penʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, literally "somethong growing about a stump"
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опёнок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opjónok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опёнка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опя́та</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опёнки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опя́т</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опенок.html>опёнков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>honey fungus (<i>Armillaria</i>), a genus of edible parasitic mushroom with a yellow cap and thin stalk that live on trees and woody shrubs, especially <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Armillaria_mellea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Armillaria mellea"><i>Armillaria mellea</i></a></span>, that usually grow in groups on tree roots, stumps, and felled trees.</li></ol>

***оперативный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вный</a> (2993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">operativ</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operatívnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>efficient, prompt, quick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> operative, surgical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вмешательство.html>вмеша́тельство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnoje</b> vmešátelʹstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">surgical intervention</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> strategical, operation(s), operational
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сводка.html>сво́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnaja</b> svódka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">operations report; summary of operations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:искусство.html>иску́сство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnoje</b> iskússtvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">minor strategy; campaign tactics</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnaja</b> grúppa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">task force</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>operation(s)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> finance</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> operational
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смета.html>сме́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnaja</b> sméta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">operating budget</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативный.html>операти́вное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:управление.html>управле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>operatívnoje</b> upravlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">daily/day-to-day management/running</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:операционный.html>операцио́нный</a> (7806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Operation</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:операционный.html>операцио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operaciónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> operating
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:операционный.html>операцио́нная</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">operaciónnaja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">operating room</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> operations</li></ol>

***опередить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опередить.html>опереди́ть</a> (7165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опередить.html>опереди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operedítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опережать.html>опережа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass ahead, to take a lead, to outstrip, to leave behind</li>
<li>to do something ahead of someone; to beat somebody to the punch</li>
<li>to outdo, to surpass</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опережавший.html>опережа́вший</a> (12847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опережавший.html>опережа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operežávšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опережать.html>опережа́ть</a> (12847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опередить.html>опереди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">operedítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опережать.html>опережа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опередить.html>опереди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pass ahead, to take a lead, to outstrip, to leave behind</li>
<li>to do something ahead of someone</li>
<li>to outdo, to surpass</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперение.html>опере́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперение.html>опере́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперение.html>опере́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперение.html>опере́ний</a></b>)

***опереться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опереться.html>опере́ться</a> (5889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опереться.html>опере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">operétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lean, to rest (on, against)</li>
<li>to rely (on), to depend on, to be guided (by)</li></ol>

***опешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опешить.html>опе́шить</a> (8988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеший.html>пе́ший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péšij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unmounted, pedestrian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original sense "to be thrown off a horse".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опешить.html>опе́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opéšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

***опираться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a> (4022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пирать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">piratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the latter being a variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to carry, move, trudge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, q. v.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опереться.html>опере́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lean, to rest (on, against)</li>
<li>to rely (on), to depend on, to be guided (by)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́йте</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кты</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Davájte <b>opirátʹsja</b> tólʹko na fákty.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let us <b>be guided</b> by facts only.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">Описанный</span> многоугольник. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
